New Cotton from Zhejiang and Anhui Arrives in Shanghai

Shanghai Bank Acts as a Wholesale Agent

Direct Sales to Factories are More Valuable

After the Shanghai Bank provided loans to farmers in various provinces and organized cotton production and sales cooperatives, new cotton from Shaanxi, Henan, Shanxi, and other provinces has begun to be shipped to Shanghai. New cotton from Zhejiang and Anhui has arrived in Shanghai. The cotton produced in Longquan Township, Yuyao, Zhejiang, is called Million Cotton and is of excellent quality. The first batch was sold by farmers of the cooperative to cotton firms in Ningbo and Shanghai, at 43 yuan per dan in Ningbo and 45 yuan per dan in Shanghai. The Shanghai Bank believes that the sale of this cotton should be sold directly to manufacturers. This time, the second batch of cotton arriving in Shanghai is being sold by the Shanghai Bank as an agent, at a price of 50 yuan per dan, which is 5 yuan more than the previous sale to cotton firms. Moreover, the market is now lower than before. Assuming that the production of Million Cotton in that township is 1,000 dan per year, the difference is a total of 10,000 yuan. The Shanghai Bank has decided that all cooperative cotton will be sold directly to manufacturers by the bank.

Chen Hang Prepares to Connect to Telephone

The Chen Hang District in Pudong, in order to facilitate communication, previously planned to connect to the Shanghai urban telephone network. Xing Zhigang, the head of the district, consulted with Chen Zixin, the municipal commissioner of Yangsi District, and made every effort to consult with the Shanghai Telephone Bureau. A satisfactory solution has now been reached. The reply from Mr. Chen is recorded below: "Regarding the case of your district requesting to connect to the urban telephone network, we have now received a letter from the Telephone Bureau, which has formulated three methods: (1) The poles and wires in the urban area will be installed by the Telephone Bureau, and the poles and wires in the county area will be installed by your district itself. A public telephone will be set up in our district and charged by the number of calls. (2) The Telephone Bureau will install the poles and wires in both the urban and county areas, and the monthly fee for users will be reduced based on the number of calls (approximately 5-6 yuan per month). (3) Long-distance calls will be charged according to long-distance telephone rates. The above three methods have been submitted to the department for approval, and will be implemented as soon as approval is obtained. Please send a map of the county area as soon as possible for surveying and planning." According to this, Mr. Xing has submitted a map and requested it to be forwarded, and is soliciting opinions from local people in the neighboring districts of Sanlintang and the central river, so that they can compile them and ask the Telephone Bureau to review and handle them. We are waiting for progress.

Wu Jiang Opens Telephone Service Along the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Line 9

The Wu Jiang Telegraph Bureau's long-distance telephone service previously only connected to Suzhou and Jiaxing, so business was not very developed. Now, the Jiangsu Long-Distance Telephone Administration has submitted a request, approved by the Ministry of Communications, to open Songjiang, Liuhe, Wu Jiang, and Pingwang for telephone service to various locations along the Beijing-Shanghai railway line, as well as Jingjiang and Nantong. All incoming and outgoing calls from these locations will be relayed through Shanghai for Songjiang, through Taicang for Liuhe, and through Suzhou for Wu Jiang and Pingwang. Operations officially commenced on the 16th, making transportation in Wu Jiang even more convenient.

Two Robbery Cases in Wuxi City and Countryside 10

Wang Kaicheng, a farmer from Wutangmen Township in the southern suburbs, lived a modest life. However, at around 6 PM the other night, six robbers suddenly arrived, armed with porcelain pistols and flashlights. They entered his home and robbed him, forbidding anyone from making a sound. Wang's wife, Hua, resisted slightly and was injured in the arm. They made off with three gold rings, three gold bangles, four gold bracelets, and silver dollars, totaling over one hundred yuan in losses. Furthermore, at the Taian Inn in Shantou Lane outside the North Gate, three violent travelers robbed the innkeeper's wife, Xu Ge, of two gold Ruyi hairpins she was wearing while she was in the room preparing tea, fleeing immediately after. Since the loss was minimal, the victim did not report to the authorities to request an investigation.

The Phenomenon of Industrial and Commercial Failure

The county used to be known as "Little Shanghai" during the heyday of silk factories. In recent years, silkworm farming has failed, silk factories have closed, rural areas have gone bankrupt, and commerce has plummeted. While commerce was still flourishing in the years 1929, 1930, 1931, and 1932, each year since 1932 has been worse than the last, and this year is the worst of all. In previous years, monthly stamp sales throughout the county could reach around 30,000 yuan. However, in recent months, monthly sales have only reached 16,000 or 17,000 yuan, a decrease of 40% compared to previous years. This is clear evidence of industrial and commercial failure.

Significant Embezzlement in Jiangyin Land Tax Case 11

Clerks within and outside the Land Tax Office of the County Government colluded to embezzle funds. After investigations by various agencies, it was discovered that over 13,000 yuan in forged payment receipts were issued within the land price tax for the 22nd year. Some of the payment receipts are still scattered among the people, and the total amount is impossible to verify. To thoroughly investigate the matter, a public notice has been issued to all grain households, requiring them to register any payment receipts they have with the Land Tax Office within one month. Expired receipts will be rendered invalid.

Drug Pill Operation Cracked in Changjing Town

The scourge of Jiangyin's "red pills" is most prevalent in Changjing, making it the hub for trafficking, selling, and consumption. The distribution of the drug pills covers the three counties of Cheng, Xi, and Qin. The red pill criminals had been skillful and organized, and the ring had never been caught. After the provincial government strictly prohibited highly addictive narcotics, local figures from the region formed a drug resistance association. Recently, a certain university graduate, Song Qixiang, and Li Guozhen, a graduate from Shanghai Academy of Fine Arts, with Li Ruibao, the wife of Shen Yu, secretly established a red pill operation. Due to uneven distribution of profits, the scheme was leaked. The drug resistance association searched the premises and found equipment and raw materials. Shen's wife, Li Ruibao, and Song Qixiang were arrested. On the 19th, they were interrogated by Cheng Shi, the magistrate. Song Qixiang and others firmly denied the charges. After summonsing witnesses, they will be handed over to the provincial garrison headquarters for further investigation.

Recent Progress on the Zhenjiang-Chengjiang Road Project 12

The Wuben section of the Zhenjiang-Chengjiang Road has already been completed. The Highway Administration Office of the Construction Bureau has transported five large vehicles and dispatched personnel to Changzhou to establish a Zhenjiang-Chengjiang Road Transportation Office to commence passenger service. It is reported that the Highway Administration Office is pushing to complete the Mengben section (from Benniu to Menghe) of the road, and has ordered its completion within a limited time, with a scheduled opening date of the 25th of this month.

Bandits Kill and Rob in Qingjiang 13

Yu Yuanfa, 32, from Taiping Lane east of Shuangqigan outside Huaiyin City, recently opened a fat pig business in Xiaozhangji, Lianshui. Yesterday (the 18th), he went to Pu to collect funds and was returning to Lianshui with silver dollars at noon. While traveling through the Majia Dadian area, about four or five li from Pu, he was suddenly intercepted by bandits. In addition to stealing over 1,000 yuan in cash that he was carrying, they shot Yuanfa with three bullets to the head, causing him to die instantly from his injuries. It was truly tragic.

Nantung District in Nantong Purges Hidden Bandits 14

Due to rampant banditry in the six counties of the Nantong District (Tong, Ru, Hai, Chong, Qi, and Jing), the district headquarters has ordered the six counties to immediately dispatch security teams to conduct a joint household registration check with the district head to arrest hidden bandits and strictly suppress transient migrants from other regions to eliminate the source of bandits. To prevent bandits from fleeing from one area to another during suppression efforts, Commander Zheng issued a joint suppression certificate, without territorial restrictions.

Large Sum of Money Lost on a Bus

Li Guangbing, a student at Nantong Middle School, was traveling from Rugao to Tong on Su-Character No. 735 bus, carrying a package containing 1,800 yuan in cash entrusted to him by a relative. He handed it to the bus driver, Pan Hesheng, only stating that it contained peanuts and tied it to the outside footboard. It was lost on the way, leading to a dispute. On the 20th, the case was reported to the Public Security Bureau and transferred to the court. Pan Hesheng was detained after interrogation.

Suining People's Education Center Sponsors Credit Cooperative 15

Director Fu of the County Relief Institute once raised 1,000 yuan to organize a loan office to aid the poor, lending sums ranging from three or four yuan to ten yuan at a monthly interest rate of six percent. This was considered convenient by the general population of the poor. However, such small and short-term loans only benefited small vendors in the urban area and did not reach farmers. Recently, Zhu Bohong, the director of the County People's Education Center, initiated a solicitation of honest farmers and guided the organization of a credit cooperative to facilitate financial turnover. The People's Education Center is also responsible for borrowing from banks and providing guarantees. Currently, the cooperatives that have been approved for establishment in various districts include San Yangzhuang and Xiao Haozhuang in Guanwang Township, Wangzhuang in Gaozuo Town, Pancun in Pancun Township, Zhangcun in Heping Township, Zhaizhuang in Hequ Township, and Maqiaozhuang in the Eighth District. Others, such as Zhan Cheng, are also in preparation. The county government has issued separate instructions to revise any parts of the cooperative organizations that do not comply with the new provincial regulations.

Hangzhou: Thirty People Poisoned by Rice Flour Balls 16

Chen Songlin, of No. 8, Dangpu Lane, Jinzhi Temple Lane, Hangzhou, was holding a wedding for his son, Chen Zixue, who is 27 years old and works as a fortune teller. Chen Zixue is blind. He was marrying A'er, the daughter of Yu Fengxiang of No. 119, Pishi Lane, who is also blind and works as a fortune teller. They came together as fellow apprentices. Yesterday (the 20th) was the wedding day. The bride's family ordered a large batch of green rice flour balls from Ruan Shunxing Rice Cake Shop in Lianqiao. They were delivered to the groom's house at 9 AM. The groom's family distributed the green rice flour balls to the neighbors, two or three to each household, and kept ten to send back to the bride's family, also distributing them to their neighbors. However, after eating the rice flour balls, everyone complained of stomach pain and vomiting. A total of thirty people were poisoned. They all complained to the bride's family and the rice cake shop, and reported the incident to the Public Security Bureau, which sent the poisoned people to the Municipal Hospital for treatment. According to the doctors, the poisoning was caused by food coloring. While the lighter cases were not life-threatening, eating too much could be dangerous. The Public Security Bureau has detained all the families and the owner of the rice cake shop for investigation.

International Commercial Telegrams 17

—Reuter's Special Commercial News, November 21—

Gold and Silver

British Gold: The London gold price today was 139 shillings and 5.5 pence, 2 pence lower than yesterday's price.

British Silver: The London silver market was stable today. The spot price was 24 pence and 4375, and the futures price was 24 pence and 5625, both up 1875. Trading was light, with both India and speculators buying.

American Silver: The Mountrie silver market saw futures rise by 10 to 15 points. The trend is expected to continue upwards.

Indian Silver: The Bombay silver market was stable today. The losses from yesterday were recovered. The closing spot price was 66 rupees and 11 annas, up 8 annas.

Exchange Rates

British-American: The London foreign exchange market was slightly more active today. The opening exchange rate for British pounds to American dollars was $4.984375, 1875 lower than yesterday's closing rate. The pound rose during the morning, and the price at 2 PM was $4.990625, up 625 from the opening price. Also, one American dollar was equivalent to 4 shillings and 0090 British gold. British-French: The opening price was 75 francs and 68, up 6 points. It continued to rise by 3 points, then remained unchanged.

American-British: The New York foreign exchange market saw a slight stabilization of the British pound today. The opening exchange rate for American dollars to British pounds was up 375, at $4.99. It soon fell by 125, to $4.98875. Afterwards, the exchange market was stable and unchanged.

Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: The cotton market was quiet and lackluster due to the weakness of the wheat market and favorable weather reports. The opening price fell by 3-4 points. Prices then recovered slightly due to purchases from Liverpool and demand from colleagues. Trading was limited and unremarkable. The market situation is easily affected. The ginning report estimates that a total of 8,633,000 bales of new cotton were ginned before November 14th. This figure had little impact on the cotton market. The ginning figure for October 31st was 7,920,000 bales.

Indian Cotton: The Bombay cotton market initially rose due to purchases by exchange operators and short covering. It then fell due to unfavorable news from Liverpool and profit-taking by bulls. The price of white Luo cotton for the April-May term was 216 rupees and 25, up one rupee from yesterday.

British Cotton: The cotton market eased slightly. At 1 PM, the price for the January term was 6.58, down 4 points.

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market plummeted today. At 1 PM, the price for the December term was 4 shillings and 6 pence and 625, down 1 penny and 375.

American Wheat: The Chicago wheat price fell sharply due to concerns that French wheat would be dumped in the US, combined with favorable weather reports and news of a weak overseas wheat market. There was a lot of closing for the December term. The opening price fell by 875.

Rubber

London: The rubber market was calm today. The trading price for the January-February term at noon was 6 points and 25, the same as yesterday's price.

New York: The rubber market opened down 4-5 points, but soon recovered.

Securities

New York: Wall Street expected the securities market to be stable and sluggish this morning. Unfavorable labor-management relations caused considerable anxiety, but if the report to be released today by American Telephone & Telegraph Co. proves to be satisfactory, the market situation can be expected to be lively. Before the opening of securities trading this morning, the factors favorable to the market situation were: (1) The pressure on public utility stocks has gradually shown signs of exhaustion; (2) The number of shares sold during price declines continues to decrease; (3) Although market price fluctuations have been recently uncertain, market commentators are mostly bullish; (4) Chicago steel mill output accounts for 33% of production capacity, an increase of two points compared to before. The factors unfavorable to the market situation are: the lack of driving force, the bearishness of the wheat market is also disturbing, and (5) public investors remain few. The securities market opened stable this morning, with very small price fluctuations and active trading. The atmosphere is pleasant and shows signs of progress. The various market prices are as follows:

Following the Exchange of Ambassadors Between China and Turkey

Negotiations for a Sino-Turkish Commercial Treaty

He Yaozu Can Present Proposals for Signing Upon Taking Office Next Month

Shen Shi News Agency reports that after the Sino-Turkish Treaty of Friendship was concluded on April 4, 1934, by our Ambassador to Switzerland, Hu Shize, on behalf of the government, in the Turkish capital with Turkish Foreign Minister Rushdi, the treaty was reviewed and approved by our Legislative Yuan on May 26 of this year. The Turkish government ratified the treaty on June 4 and it took effect on September 1. Recently, our government officially appointed He Yaozu as the first ambassador to Turkey and he is scheduled to depart for Turkey to assume his post at the beginning of next month. The Turkish ambassador to China has also been appointed. According to sources in diplomatic circles, after the establishment of diplomatic relations between China and Turkey, the two sides are preparing to negotiate a Sino-Turkish commercial treaty. The signing of this commercial treaty is urgently needed by the overseas Chinese communities in both countries. Overseas Chinese in Turkey, including Ma Hongdao and Wang Zengshan, have repeatedly petitioned our Ministry of Foreign Affairs to expedite the signing of the commercial treaty to facilitate business in foreign countries. In view of this, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is actively deliberating the matter. After Ambassador He Yaozu arrives in Turkey, the issue of the commercial treaty will be formally presented to the Turkish government for negotiation and signing at an early date. According to customs reports, the current state of trade between China and Turkey in 1933 saw China's imports at approximately 4,800 yuan and exports at 52,300 yuan. However, these figures only refer to maritime trade. Due to geographical reasons, Sino-Turkish trade relies more on land trade, so the volume of trade between China and Turkey is still considerable and has been developing rapidly this year. It is expected that international trade between China and Turkey will make significant progress after the Sino-Turkish commercial treaty is formally signed.

Swedish Envoy to Arrive in Nanjing Next Week

Office of Foreign Affairs Notified Yesterday

But No Definite Date of Departure Yet

Central News Agency reports that Swedish Minister to China and Japan, Mr. Folke Mannerheim, arrived in China from Japan on the 19th to inspect overseas Chinese affairs. Yesterday morning, he dispatched Consul Hardmok to visit Yu Ming, Director of the Office of Foreign Affairs of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Shanghai, to inform him that the Swedish Envoy is scheduled to arrive in Nanjing within the next week to visit Foreign Minister Wang. However, the exact date of departure has not yet been determined.

Nicaraguan Vice President to Visit Nanjing Tonight

Paid a Visit to Mayor Wu Yesterday Morning

Mayor Wu Returned the Visit

Dr. Espinoza, Vice President of Nicaragua, arrived in Shanghai from Japan on the 19th and stayed at the International Hotel. He was originally scheduled to visit Nanjing yesterday morning, but due to his visit to Mayor Wu, he will now leave Shanghai for Nanjing at 11 PM tonight to visit our government officials, with the aim of strengthening friendly relations between the two countries. In addition to requesting the Railway Bureau to provide a special decorated train, the municipal government will have Mayor Wu and others personally see him off at the station, and dispatch police detectives to maintain order and a military band to bid him farewell. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has specially assigned Lin Xiangshi, Section Chief of Protocol, to arrive in Shanghai this morning to accompany Mr. Espinoza to Nanjing. After visiting our government officials in Nanjing, Mr. Espinoza will travel to Beiping on the 25th to visit various scenic spots, and then return south at the beginning of next month. On the 4th, he will take a boat to visit Xiaoluzong and other places before returning to his country.

Visit to Mayor Wu: The Vice President of Nicaragua, accompanied by the Honorary Consul of Nicaragua and several attendants, visited Mayor Wu at the Municipal Government in the city center at 11 AM yesterday. The municipal government had pre-arranged a guard of honor and a military band to stand on both sides of the steps in front of the Municipal Government to welcome them. After Mr. Espinoza and his party arrived at the Municipal Government and disembarked, the guard of honor presented arms and the military band played music. Mayor Wu, accompanied by Secretaries Geng Jiaji and Tang Shixuan, personally welcomed them at the steps and escorted them to the Mayor's Reception Room, where they were treated with champagne. The guests and hosts had a pleasant conversation for about ten minutes before Mr. Espinoza departed. Mayor Wu personally escorted him to the gate, where the guard of honor again presented arms and the military band played music to bid him farewell.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: The weather around Shandong is clear and cold, with northwest winds. The middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River are cloudy and cold, with fog in the morning. The wind comes from varying directions between northwest and northeast. The East China Sea is overcast with rain and has northeast winds. Jiangxi has low pressure. Furthermore, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the temperature in this city reached a high of 54.0 and a low of 45.5. On the same day last year, the high was 74.3 and the low was 44.6.

Kindergarten Textbooks

Previous Approvals Invalid

The Municipal Education Bureau yesterday instructed municipal private primary and secondary schools, kindergartens, and bookstores in this city, stating, "In accordance with the Ministry of Education's Instruction No. 130000, it is found that the formal standards for the curricula of kindergartens, primary schools, and junior and senior high schools have been promulgated by the Ministry successively, and all bookstores have been notified to comply with these formal standards in compiling primary and secondary school textbooks. The primary and secondary school textbooks compiled by various bookstores in accordance with the provisional standards for primary and secondary school curricula before the promulgation of these formal standards, regardless of whether they were approved by the former University Council or the Ministry, except for the parts of the third year of junior and senior high school that are currently in use, may still be used, but all other books should be invalid from the date of this announcement, and schools shall not use them. Until the textbooks for a certain subject used by each middle school can be purchased from the various bookstores that have been recently approved by the Ministry, they are allowed to temporarily compile their own lecture notes as a substitute, but they must comply with the formal curriculum standards for each subject and still submit all teaching materials to the Ministry for review at the end of each semester, except for separate orders. It is hereby ordered that the Bureau forward this order to all primary and secondary schools and bookstores under its jurisdiction to comply with it." In addition to separate orders, it is hereby ordered that they comply with it.

Called a Meeting Yesterday to Evaluate Grades

National Shanghai College of Commerce First

Pan Youqiang, Director of the Training Headquarters, inspected the military training of schools in Jiangsu, Shanghai, Zhejiang, and Fujian this time. The main points of the evaluation were as follows: (1) School aspect: A. Schools should follow the government's intentions, assist the instructors, and strive for the progress of military training. B. Schools should enrich the military training equipment according to the "Minimum Equipment List for Military Education" promulgated by the Ministry. C. The school administration should urge students to wear uniforms uniformly. (2) Instructor aspect: A. Instructors should maintain close contact with the school authorities. B. Instructors should pay attention to the essentials of command and the method of teaching. C. Instructors should strictly abide by the implementation of mutual assistance methods. D. Instructors should abide by the implementation of the average salary method. (3) Colleges and universities with excellent results: National Shanghai College of Commerce won first place. It is said that Principal Fei Fuheng usually strongly promotes military training, the instructors guide well, the teaching methods are appropriate, the students are full of energy, their movements are accurate, and the discipline is strict, so they can have such excellent results. Shanghai Municipal Council's Chinese Education Funding

Over 1.8 Million Yuan This Year

The Chinese school portion of the Shanghai Municipal Council's education funding has recently been reported in the newspapers, but not in detail. According to investigations, the Municipal Council's budget for this year (1934) includes administrative expenses for four Chinese boys' middle schools and one Chinese girls' middle school under the education expenses, which, after offsetting the tuition income of over 213,000 yuan, still require an expenditure of over 417,000 yuan. In addition, the expenses for five Chinese children's primary schools and the Chinese Education Department, after offsetting tuition fees of over 41,000 yuan, still require an expenditure of over 196,000 yuan. Furthermore, the cost of purchasing stationery and other items for primary and secondary schools totals over 31,000 yuan, the cost of repairing school buildings is over 64,000 yuan, and various miscellaneous expenses, including staff pension subsidies, rent, sanitation, inspection expenses, student physical examination expenses, free places, and accounting expenses, total over 101,000 yuan. The interest on real estate investment is over 213,000 yuan. In addition, the subsidies for private schools total 188,950 yuan. The above totals over 1.21 million yuan in recurring expenses. As for the temporary expenses, there are 300,800 yuan for the purchase of land for the Huade Road Primary School, 280,000 yuan for the continued allocation of construction funds for the Chinese Girls' Middle School, and 27,000 yuan for the new heating equipment for the Nie Zhongcheng Public School and the construction of walls for the Chinese Children's Public School. The total of recurring and temporary expenditures is over 1.832 million yuan. The Shanghai Municipal Council's education budget totals over 3.377 million yuan this year, of which approximately 54% is directly used for Chinese schools.

Education Bureau Issues

Middle School Student Registration Form Style

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau yesterday instructed all secondary schools, stating, "In investigating student registration, the school should have detailed records of the student's educational experience, the registration process, and the Bureau's review situation, so that it can be easily checked and reviewed from time to time to avoid errors. In the past, schools have often not paid attention to this, resulting in students being rejected upon graduation because the procedures were not met, and the schools were still at a loss and did not know why. The impact is not small. In view of this, in order to remedy this situation, the Bureau has formulated a type of student registration form for self-use by schools, which schools should imitate and apply. However, if the original method is indeed excellent, it can also be used as a reference to achieve perfection, and it must be completed within one month of the arrival of the document. The Bureau will send personnel to the school for spot checks at any time, and all shall comply." This order is accompanied by a sample of the student registration form for self-use by schools.

Education and Public Safety Bureaus Proclamation

Underground Exposed Antiquities Belong to the State

Those Who Conceal and Fail to Report Will Be Prosecuted for Theft

The Education and Public Safety Bureaus of this city, under orders, announced that antiquities exposed from the ground should belong to the state. Those who conceal and fail to report will be prosecuted for theft. The joint proclamation is recorded below: "In accordance with the Municipal Government's Instruction No. 11463, 'In accordance with the Ministry of Interior's Consultation No. 238, "Article 7 of the Antiquities Preservation Law stipulates that 'Antiquities buried underground or exposed from underground shall belong to the state.' When the aforementioned antiquities are discovered, the discoverer shall immediately report to the local competent administrative authority, which shall submit them to the superior agency to consult the Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Interior and the Central Antiquities Preservation Committee for the storage of the antiquities and grant a considerable bonus. Those who fail to report and conceal will be prosecuted for theft," etc. This matter has been consulted to the subordinate agencies for faithful compliance in June of the 21st year of the Republic. However, recently, newspapers have reported that antiquities are discovered from time to time in various places, and some have been bought by antiquities dealers. In this way, there is no negligence in the responsibility of preserving antiquities. It is proposed that your Municipal Government instruct its subordinates to thoroughly investigate and make a list when antiquities are discovered within its jurisdiction and handle it in accordance with the previous law, and re-announce the reporting procedures for general knowledge, except for separate consultations, and it should be consulted for compliance and reply."'" In accordance with this, in addition to the order from this Public Safety Bureau to its subordinates to comply, it is hereby announced for general knowledge, and all shall comply without violation.

China Science Society

Biological Institute Obtains Strange Fish

▲ The Whole Body is Red and Green Like a Parrot

The Biological Institute of the China Science Society collects countless specimens of various plants and animals from home and abroad, of which fish account for half of the total. Previously, the institute sent Wang Yikang and others to join various academic groups to form the Hainan Biology Collection Group to collect fish specimens on Qiong Island. A strange fish was discovered on the island, with its whole body like a parrot, appearing red and green. Its eyes are protruding like spheres, as beautiful as the eyes of a parrot. It is now on display at the institute, and various biological experts are invited to verify its name.

Sports News 24

Fudan Wins Jiangda Cross-Country Championship

Fudan First with 57 Points, Central Second with 69 Points

Individual First: Dong Shuzhao from Guanghua, 22 Minutes 25.4 Seconds

Today's All-Around Competition Begins

The Jiangda Athletic Association's cross-country championship was held yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM at Chih Tze University in Jiangwan. Only five schools participated: Central, Jinling, Fudan, Guanghua, and Chih Tze. Interest was less than in previous years. As a result of the competition, Fudan University won the championship with 57 points, Central came in second, Guanghua third, Jinling fourth, and Chih Tze, as the host, came in last. The individual first place went to Dong Shuzhao of Guanghua, with a time of 22 minutes, 25 and 5/2 seconds. The entire course was 6,900 meters. The Jiangda all-around competition will also be held this afternoon and tomorrow afternoon at Chih Tze University.

▲ Scores of Each School

(2nd, 4th, 7th, 11th, 16th, 17th)

(2) Central University 69 points

(3rd, 6th, 9th, 12th, 19th, 20th)

(3) Guanghua University 71 points

(1st, 10th, 13th, 14th, 15th, 18th)

(4) Jinling University 126 points

(5th, 21st, 22nd, 24th, 25th, 29th)

▲ A Glimpse of the Competition

Fudan's victory relied entirely on the evenness of its talent. The three major generals, Yang, Lan, and Liu, ranked among the top. Although Dong Shuzhao of Guanghua won the individual first place, one pillar cannot support a collapsing building. The entire course was 6,900 meters long, starting in front of the Chih Tze gate, going along the Water and Electricity Road, passing the Baziqiao Bridge, entering Tongji Road, Jiangwan Road, Xinshi Road, returning to Water and Electricity Road, and returning to the Chih Tze gate. After the 30 competitors started, veteran Dong Shuzhao immediately took the lead. However, the ten behind him were generally not far apart, separated by only a few meters. Upon reaching the finish line, Dong Shuzhao was still first. The runner-up, Yang Qingxie, was more than twenty meters behind, and Wang Dayao of Central was another twenty meters behind. After about ten meters, another competitor arrived, and the distances gradually increased thereafter, until the last person.

▲ All-Around Competition

Shen Bao National Products Weekly

Contributions

Remembering Mr. Shi Liangcai 25

— Editor

Speaking of national products, we cannot but remember Mr. Shi Liangcai. After the "September 18th" and "January 28th" incidents, the Chinese people frowned and gnashed their teeth, wanting to find a way to avenge themselves and wipe out the shame. It can be said that this accounted for the majority of the population. But empty talk of revenge and wiping out the shame is of course useless. At that time, Mr. Shi, in the local association, convened a meeting with various gentlemen to discuss the idea of arousing the people's attention to using national products. It was specifically designated that the 22nd year of the Republic of China would be the National Products Year. A National Products Weekly was specially created in the Shen Bao to advocate and promote it. He specially instructed the editor and Mr. Du Chongyuan to preside over the editing. Mr. Shi inquired and encouraged us every time we met. At the end of last year, he convened another meeting at the local association. Because women have a greater responsibility for using national products, this year was officially designated as the Women's National Products Year. He also instructed the editor to visit and specially commend those who have made practical contributions to the national products business and those who have succeeded in the industrial world after arduous struggles, so that the national products industry would have hope for progress. This year, which has been designated as the Women's National Products Year, Mr. Shi also instructed us to interview female leaders and enthusiastic women about their opinions on national products for the reference of the national products industry. Mr. Shi wholeheartedly supported and encouraged the editor in any requests made to him regarding national products companies and factories, so that they would be successful. I still remember a few days before Mr. Shi went to Hangzhou, the editor went to the newspaper office at Mr. Shi's invitation to talk. Mr. Shi said that promoting national products should be considered from the National Products Year itself. What are the difficulties in the national products industry? What are the obstacles to the national products industry? How many shortcomings should be addressed? How many advantages should be imitated? What are the reasons why they cannot compete with foreign goods? All of these should be investigated on the ground and disclosed completely so that the people would have the opportunity to think of ways to address them. Therefore, a special investigation record of the national products industry was added to the newspaper for the research of those who care about the national products business. Such enthusiasm, perseverance, vision, and insight for the struggle and labor for the national products industry is worth remembering and cherishing. Although Mr. Shi is dead, Mr. Shi's spirit is not dead, Mr. Shi's doctrine is not dead, and the warmth of Mr. Shi's advocacy of national products must be continued and carried forward by those of us who are still alive to comfort Mr. Shi's spirit in heaven.

Talking About National Products

Let's Build a Mentality of Loving and Using National Products 26

— Wei Taishun

The voice of promoting national products has now been heard by almost everyone: opening the newspaper, there are texts promoting national products every day; national products organizations are also thinking about ways to encourage the use of national products all day long; ladies and gentlemen who are enthusiastic about national products in society are also making various national products promotions at any time with parched lips and tongues; however, the facts are in front of us, and in the past six months, the country's money has still been flowing out drop by drop. What is the reason for this?

If we want to save the country wholeheartedly, and if we want to stop the leakage of money, we must first see how other countries perished. In the past, those who destroyed other people's countries used politics or military affairs, but now it is not always the case. The most recent weapon to destroy other people's countries is a deadly economy; economics is really a gun, a cannon, and poisonous gas that kills people without shedding blood. We see one East India Company that can end the huge country of India. From this, we can infer that we are really not afraid of guns, cannons, and poisonous gas. We are not afraid of elite troops. What we really need to be afraid of is the beautiful and attractive foreign goods that squeeze our beloved people's wealth and blood!

If we want money not to overflow, of course, Chinese people must love and use Chinese goods, and fight against foreign goods. If money does not flow out, the country's economy will naturally be very prosperous. But it is strange to say that we know that using foreign goods is enough to destroy other people's countries, so why does the report of the International Trade Bureau still show an increase in import surplus? Why is it that the food and clothing of the Chinese people are still mostly foreign goods? I think there must still be thousands of people with the following eight mentalities:

(1) Using foreign goods is beautiful, and it can show my wealth, fashion, modernity, and ease.

(2) What does my individual use of foreign goods have to do with the national economy, let alone the survival of the country.

(3) Even if there are substitutes for foreign goods, they claim that they are purchased only out of necessity.

(4) When it is discovered that they have recently bought foreign goods from foreign stores, they claim that they were bought in the past.

(5) Others are using foreign goods, so I might as well imitate them.

(6) Those who are afraid of losing their status by using national products have to wear a set of national products clothes to cover up when there is a gathering.

(7) Foreign goods are cheaper and of better quality than Chinese goods, so why should I buy expensive and inferior Chinese goods.

(8) I cannot distinguish between Chinese and foreign goods. As long as they fit my material desires, they are all good.

If the Chinese people have the above eight mentalities, how can national products have hope of getting out of trouble, and how can the national economy have a prosperous day? We should start from today. All those who have a patriotic heart must grit their teeth and take responsibility to work hard, work hard, and work until everyone loves and uses national products, feels that using foreign goods is a shame, and using national products is an honor. Gradually, we should eliminate the mentality of using foreign goods and build a mentality of loving and using national products. Based on the mentality of loving and using national products, we should start from our own families, and slowly spread it to all compatriots in the country. Everyone should put it into practice, so that it is as if we have built a solid fortress, and even if foreign goods with beautiful faces come to attack and lure us, we will absolutely not fall for their tricks. But how should we build a mentality of loving and using national products? At least three conditions must be met:

(1) Self-confidence and self-esteem We trust that we are patriotic citizens. We must first fundamentally understand the advantages and disadvantages of using foreign goods and national products, and believe that loving and using national products is unique, and buying foreign goods is base and shameless. The most glorious and prestigious thing in the world is the use of national products. Creating a love for national products is the secret to increasing prestige, and everyone will respect him.

(2) Despise Westernization We should respect those who love and use national products. On the other hand, we should despise those who wear foreign goods. From now on, if there are Westernized people coming, we will scoff at them and avoid them. Over time, those who use foreign goods may feel ashamed and change their habits.

(3) Strive for self-improvement Foreign goods are a weapon to destroy other people's countries, so we should immediately turn around, strive for self-improvement, start from now, cherish our money, and set our goals to do the patriotic work of loving and using national products.

Discussion on National Products

How to Avoid "Intra-Industry Competitive Selling" 27

— Xiao Bai

——A Major Issue Facing National Products

At present, if we talk about the issue of national products, no one will forget the two sharp knives that destroy the life of national products and hinder the progress of national products - one is foreign goods from abroad, and the other is the products produced by foreign factories in China, which are considered to be the objects that urgently need to be eliminated for the future development of national products. However, aside from this, who knows that, on the other hand, national products factories themselves are also "drinking poison to quench their thirst", suffering from an extremely serious terminal illness, whose crisis and impact is really "more than" the former two. This is - "intra-industry competitive selling". Originally, this evil demon, at present, with the economic panic and the downturn in the market, is extremely active in the current national products industry, which is worth discussing.

We know that "intra-industry competitive selling", although it is said to be an inevitable thing under intense commercial warfare and free trade, however, in our country, because there are no reasonable sanctions and the concept of selfishness among Chinese people is too deep, regardless of the overall plan, its rampantness is increasingly out of control. Recently, because of the drought in the south and the flood in the north, the whole country is suffering from disasters, the rural economy is accelerating its collapse, and purchasing power is weakening day by day, which affects the decline in sales of national products, resulting in overproduction, so prices are falling more and more. Moreover, it also manufactures substandard goods to cater to customers' psychology, which confuses, darkens and disrupts the market. As far as I know, at present, there are already a few emerging industries whose selling prices are even lower than the cost price, not to mention others. This phenomenon and this situation is a big problem in the future of revitalizing national products, and it must be solved quickly. Now, I dare to offer my opinion and list the two steps of temporary treatment below:

(1) Set Prices First, various trade associations should quickly convene a general meeting of members, discuss and agree on price regulations, abide by them together, and have each factory submit a certificate of deposit and publicly disclose the sales accounts, so that the association can check them at any time. If there is any violation, the certificate of deposit will be confiscated.

(2) Eliminate Substandard Goods Cutting corners and selling substandard goods is also a way for the national products industry to decline on its own. In this crisis, the association must notify all factories to urgently eliminate them, no longer manufacture them, and strive to reduce the cost of genuine goods and lower the selling price to benefit the public.

Although, the fundamental solution lies in the self-awareness and thorough feeling of the national products industry itself, we must know that "intra-industry competition" is tantamount to a "suicide policy", especially in the era when China's industry is still in its infancy. This "mutual trampling" will inevitably "hurt both sides", and "the snipe and clam fight", the Western fishermen are showing their ferocious smiles and intensifying their work, trying to profit from it.

Suggestions for Organizing a National Products Propaganda Team 28

— Wang Shouqiu

Students Use Spare Time on Weekends

To Conduct In-Depth Propaganda in Rural Villages

Promoting national products and using national products is very easy to shout out, but putting it into practice is the opposite of very easy, and becomes very difficult. Therefore, whether it is the National Products Year or the Women's National Products Year, foreign goods still flow in like water; and our country's money? It flows out like water: although it is the same flow, foreigners flow with smiles, while Chinese people? On the contrary, they flow with sallow faces and thin bodies, frowning and glaring! Under this situation, of course, we must reverse the flow of money outward, so that it flows upstream and into the pockets of our Chinese people!

Anyone knows that promoting national products is the responsibility and obligation of citizens, but why is it that promoting national products does not work? Why is there still a leakage of tens of millions of yuan every year? Is the heart of the Chinese people really dead? Is the blood of the Chinese people really cold? I don't think so; because 80-90% of Chinese people have not received education, and if people who have not received education are not explained to them, how do they know to promote national products? Moreover, even those who have received education cannot recognize whether goods are national products or not, so that they are deceived. This is also a common occurrence. Therefore, I think we need to expand propaganda, and we need oral propaganda—oral propaganda and written propaganda, both are equally important, because oral propaganda is propaganda for illiterate people, and written propaganda is propaganda for literate people, so neither can be abandoned. —The purpose of propaganda is (1) to promote the meaning of national products; (2) to distinguish the common sense of national products; for the propagandists of oral propaganda, it is best to ask students to serve. Because they can use their spare time on weekends to organize "National Products Propaganda Teams" to go deep into the people and into the countryside to carry out propaganda. I think: this will definitely receive great results! I hope that students from all schools will come to serve this kind of propaganda work, so that the Women's National Products Year will achieve final victory!

National Products Survey

Domestic Goods in Wenzhou 29

— Hu Feng

(Wenzhou Correspondence) Wenzhou, in the eyes of the average person, may seem like a place not worth paying attention to. But in terms of cigarettes alone, the annual consumption reaches about three to four million yuan.

Wenzhou used to have six counties, sometimes referred to as the six counties of Wenzhou, and that's from an administrative point of view. However, from a commercial point of view, Wenzhou actually includes the six counties belonging to the upper reaches of the Ou River (Chuzhou). So, although Wenzhou is a small trading port, its total import and export trade is still sufficient to occupy a considerable position among China's trading ports.

According to past years' statistics, Wenzhou's trade has always been in deficit. This is because Wenzhou's production exports are small each year, while the imports of consumables are large. Among these many consumables, there are two conditions that meet the psychological requirements of the people of Wenzhou:

First, the price must be cheap:

Second, the designs must be novel.

There are indeed domestic goods that meet the above two conditions, but there are definitely not many of them. Moreover, when foreign goods are being dumped in our country on a large scale, how many things in the market can compete with foreign goods after all? Therefore, the future of domestic goods in Wenzhou is bound to have little hope.

At present, for the sake of implementing the New Life Movement, the general public is temporarily stirred by enthusiasm, and organizations such as anti-Japanese associations and domestic goods promotion associations are emerging in response. At the same time, the Shanghai China National Products Company has also established a large store of China National Products Company in Wenzhou as a branch, and it actually officially opened on October 10th. Mr. Wang Zhenfang and Mr. Wang Xingyao were sent from Shanghai to Wenzhou to provide guidance. It is said that recent business has been developing very well. What will happen in the future? Of course, I cannot be dogmatic. But if prices can be cheap and designs can be novel, if such things are sold in large quantities at the Wenzhou China National Products Company, then I can guarantee that this company will definitely be able to exist permanently in Wenzhou. Otherwise, five minutes will pass, and the Wenzhou China National Products Company may also pass with those five minutes!

Blue cloth shirts were once all the rage in Wenzhou, but what about now? This is enough to prove what the future holds for domestic goods in Wenzhou!

Domestic Goods News

A Record of the Opening of the National Goods Exhibition in Penglai Market 30

— Sun Choucheng

The opening of the 6th National Goods Movement Conference of this city on the anniversary of the birth of Premier Sun Yat-sen has two meanings: (1) to commemorate the sage who created the Republic of China, and (2) to hope that all compatriots in the country will follow the Premier's nation-building plan and strive for material construction in order to save the dying national economy. This is also good news within the Women's National Goods Year. I am recording what I have seen in this publication, hoping it will be noted by comrades who promote national goods.

The venue is located in the Penglai Night Garden at the south end of Penglai Market, Xiaoximen, in this city. A towering pine and cypress archway is erected at the entrance. After signing in, guests are given the "China National Goods Survey Booklet" compiled by the Shanghai National Goods Introduction and Reporting Office, and the "Special Issue" published by the conference, for reference. One lists the trademarks and addresses of domestic goods factories, and the other details the various purposes and methods of promoting domestic goods, both of which are useful publications in the domestic goods industry. On the stage is a large cream cake donated by Taikang Company, more than a foot in diameter, decorated with the eight characters "Patriotic People Advocate National Goods", and stating "Respectfully Presented by Taikang Company", all made of sugar, containing artistic ideas and also advertising properties, which can be described as doing everything possible to promote. The stage is covered with chrysanthemums planted by the Municipal Garden, colorful and exceptionally beautiful. The four walls are plastered with slogans such as "Promoting domestic goods is the fundamental way to resist economic aggression" and "Using domestic goods is the only way out for the Chinese nation." China Pharmaceutical Salt Factory is distributing its products on the spot, saying that regular use of medicinal salt can prevent illness. Yu Hongjun, Secretary-General of the Municipal Government, reported on the purpose of the conference, dividing the amount of money flowing out this year due to the habit of using foreign goods into different categories, detailing them completely, saying that countries around the world are striving to develop commerce, dumping their surplus goods into our country, exchanging our money for the manufacture of weapons, speaking painfully, hoping that all compatriots across the country will quickly wake up and switch to using domestic goods in order to plug the leaks, and also hoping that manufacturers will strive to improve the quality of domestic goods and lower prices in order to counter foreign goods and save profits, his words were earnest and moving. Xu Peihuang, Director of the Public Works Bureau, said that the city holds a national goods movement conference once a year, pessimists say that the customs trade book is still in deficit, which does not help, and only wastes money to join the fun, optimists say that through this reminder, the number of people who like to use foreign goods and switch to domestic goods is increasing day by day, which is of some help to various domestic goods factories, advising domestic goods manufacturers to intensify their publicity efforts, and citing the visit to a certain cloth factory in Wuxi, where they learned that there are also such fine and beautiful fabrics among domestic goods, as proof. Ms. Lin Kecong wore a blue silk cheongsam on the day and gave a speech citing the story of a British cloth factory asking women to buy a cloth skirt each to maintain the livelihoods of workers, and advised Shanghai women to switch to domestic goods as a guide for women across the country, her words were quite sincere. Wang Jie'an of the China National Goods Maintenance Association spoke in the soft language of Wu Nong, comparing imported goods to national goods as grand cuisine to home-cooked meals, advising compatriots across the country not to go to grand restaurants every day to eat grand cuisine, resulting in bankruptcy, but rather to eat home-cooked meals at home to preserve family property, gesticulating while speaking, vivid and lively, like a storyteller, winning a lot of applause. The temporary commercial market is located on the open space in the western part of Penglai Market, with as many as 139 participating manufacturers, with all kinds of goods available. Because it was not ready on this day, the opening was changed to the next day.

Spring and Autumn

Little Western Paradise 31

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 5 Smilingly Meet and Greet, Lighting Lamps to Illuminate Withered Faces, Hungry Stomachs Drive One to Apply Powder and Learn Flirtation

Sister-in-law Hu curled her lips and said: "Oh! What are you boasting about? My family certainly doesn't have West Gate water, and your family may not have it either, right? This is other people's water, you're taking advantage of it, working here and having it to drink every day..." As she said this, she saw the Class A tea room attendant's face turn red, so she changed her smile and said: "I'm just joking with you, don't be angry." As she spoke, she took another cup and poured a bowl of tea, sending it to him, and laughed: "Let me return the favor with a cup." The tea room attendant wanted to keep a straight face, but couldn't, and could only smile. The Class B tea room attendant held his arms in his chest and laughed: "Sister-in-law Hu, you're being unfair." Before Sister-in-law Hu could say the second sentence, she had already poured two more cups of tea and sent them to his hands. The Class B tea room attendant took the tea and bowed slightly to her, laughing: "Sister-in-law Hu really does things powerfully, making people neither cry nor laugh." Sister-in-law Hu sighed and said: "It's not shameful to curry favor with you two, poor people should always be extra good to each other." The Class B tea room attendant laughed at the Class A tea room attendant: "Did you hear that, our Sister-in-law Hu has already built a low foundation here, and when something happens, she wants us to put in a good word." Before the Class A tea room attendant could finish speaking, Sister-in-law Hu just kept pursing her lips and winking at the two of them. When the two of them looked outside the room, it turned out that it was the two gentlemen, Zhang and Li, who had returned. Their faces were full of smiles, but not like usual. When the tea room attendant rushed to open the door, another gentleman in a long robe came in behind them. He took two steps, but looked back, and laughed: "Just come in, what's the rush?" As he spoke, he waved his hand inside. At this time, a woman in her early twenties came in, wearing a blue soft satin cheongsam, with white braids along the edges. Her black hair was slightly curled, only behind her head, obviously permed by an incompetent hairdresser. She had a long face, large eyes, and a high nose. Although she had black bangs, red rouge, and white face powder, the gaunt flesh on her cheeks could not be made more plump no matter what. (70)

Snippets 32

— (Tian Sheweng)

The German writer Leeson was extremely careless. One night, he returned home and knocked on the door to enter. His maidservant, mistaking him for someone else, replied: "Sir! The master hasn't returned yet." Leeson replied: "It doesn't matter, I'll come back tomorrow"! Saying that, he left on his own.

During the Spring and Autumn Period, there was a fool in the State of Lu who, when moving house, actually forgot his wife. This person had the same forgetfulness as the German Leeson.

But to bring the topic back; aren't there many people in the world who, for the sake of money, beauty, and power, bustle about until death without realizing it, forgetting themselves? Why should they laugh at others!

Talking About Crab Paintings 33

— Shiyuan

It is unknown when crab painting began in China. Roughly since the Song and Yuan dynasties, the style of painting from life became popular. Famous painters, in addition to figures and landscapes, often also painted insects and fish, and crabs were of course one of their subjects for painting from life. However, not many have been handed down to later generations, not as many as Emperor Huizong's eagles or Zhao Ziang's horses, which are almost everywhere. Twenty years ago, when I accompanied the embassy to France, I saw a Chinese crab painting in the Louvre in Paris, which was quite meticulous, with ancient paper and no signature, but with the seal of the imperial collection, probably a work of the Yuan or Ming dynasty, said to have been plundered by the Allied Forces during the Boxer Rebellion. In the early years of the Republic of China, I saw several small albums by Bai Yangshanren in Yuan Xiangcheng's staff, one of which was a painting of a crab, with unrestrained brushwork, truly a masterpiece, with a poem that said: "Crawling all night without ten feet, the world still says it walks sideways." It was also expressed with a purpose. Later, in an antique shop in Liulichang, I saw a painting of a crab by Zeng Yandong, with simple brushwork and sufficient spirit, inscribed: "See when you will walk sideways?" According to the owner of the shop, Zeng Yandong was forced to paint by his superiors when he was a county magistrate, and he made this satire, and was later offended because of it. During the Tongzhi reign, Zhao Beian traveled to Jian'ou as a staff member, and there were many strange marine products by the sea. Beian once painted a crab picture, with as many as twenty different kinds of crabs, from large horse crabs to small sand crabs, inscribed: "One crab is not as good as another crab." Beian's paintings were far superior to his calligraphy, but the world rarely knew it. Among contemporary painters who like to paint crabs, I admire Ma Mengrong the most, his brushwork is elegant, and he has both talent and skill. Several years ago, at an exhibition in Shanghai, I saw one of his crabs, with a poem by Ma Gongyu: "Marching in formation, wearing armor and wielding spears, originally without a belly or intestines, letting you walk sideways in the rivers and seas, you will eventually accompany orange and ginger at the wine table," which was a lament for the warlords of the time who held troops and walked sideways, and ridiculed them. Recently, I saw another crab by Mengrong, with a poem by Ma Gongyu: "It's another day to hold crabs and admire chrysanthemums, recalling the days when we composed poems and painted together, Rongzhai is desolate and suddenly a year has passed, and reading this picture makes tears surge forth!" I heard that Mengrong returned to the mountain not long after January 28th, and I did not have the chance to meet him, which I still regret. (Not for payment)

(Du Juan notes, Mengrong's crab paintings are naturally the work of an old wheelwright. However, what I have in my collection are only two works, a cuckoo singing on a cuckoo branch and a wisteria. I regret that I cannot raise Mengrong from the ground and beg him for a painting of a gutless gentleman. Thinking about it makes my stomach ache!)

A Day's Pleasure 34

— Wo Fo

As usual: October! October in the lunar calendar can be considered the season of joy in the countryside. Because at that time, the grain is piled on the threshing floor, the rice is stored in the granary, and cotton and beans, etc., are exchanged for money or used by oneself. The problem of hunger and cold for a year can almost be solved; then, the previous "hundred days of labor" should be compensated with "a day's pleasure" to provide spiritual adjustment. Therefore, every October, people in the countryside, regardless of men, women, old or young, always have a component of joy on their expressions. However, what about now? Isn't it also October, the joyful season? But I will temporarily set aside the current reality and first describe them based on memories! Let the farmers recall the old images of happiness. I think this will be enough for the farmers to reminisce and chew on, especially in the current situation.

This is naturally a superstitious act; but farmers have no chance to go to the cinema to watch movies, let alone qualify to go to the dance hall to dance or to the golf course to play golf. Of course, they can only seek the joy they need from traditional superstitious fantasies. Therefore, a picture of farmers having fun in October in the lunar calendar is nothing more than two ways: "going out to meetings" and "doing societies"; and these two ways of having fun are both centered on welcoming gods. First, let's talk about "going out to meetings": going out to meetings is also called "competition meetings", which is to take the idol they believe in the most, gather many people to be in charge of flags, drums, and all the necessary ceremonies, and carry the idol to patrol each village for a day or more; when the village receives the idol, it must entertain the people in the meeting, and everyone takes this opportunity to chat. Therefore, not only are the people in the meeting happy at that time, but also the villagers who have no relationship, because they can take this opportunity to "watch the meeting", so they are all happy, which can simply be called "everyone is happy". As for "doing societies", the scope is smaller than "going out to meetings". When doing societies, only a few to dozens of families are united as "society friends", and a kind of idol is also entertained in the "society head's" house. At the same time, it is also a feast for the society friends to slaughter pigs and sheep; this kind of doing society contains the meaning of thanking for the harvest and praying for a good year. In fact, this is nothing more than "a hundred days of labor, a day's pleasure".

The above—going out to meetings and doing societies are of course superstitious acts, because they are superstitious acts, they should be eliminated and prohibited. But in this year when the countryside has gone bankrupt, they—the farmers work hard and toil to cultivate the land for a year, and as a result, in addition to suffering from natural and man-made disasters, they also have to pay rent and grain, which is not enough to eat a full meal or wear a warm coat: it is about to be discarded in ditches and scattered in all directions, where is there any surplus or spare money? To seek the enjoyment of this "a day's pleasure"! Therefore, this kind of superstitious act has long been unnecessary to eliminate or prohibit, and has been eliminated and prohibited by itself.

Reforming and Returning to the Right Path 35

— Shiying

Places Visited

Gazing at Tiger Hill 36

— Huoxueming

The evening sun in late autumn is too good, faintly reddening the new gravel road. A skinny horse pulls a broken cart, and we sit on the broken cart, without using our waists and feet; the scenery of the mountains and fields will naturally flow into our eyes. The smell of horse manure at the pavilion gate and the annoying tone of the car夫 soliciting business are no longer heard, and the Liuyuan Garden with its white walls also slips past. Pointing to the west, the lush green Jiechuang Law Temple on the left really looks like a riverside mountain village scene in the deep summer of Switzerland.

There are wide grasslands here, bordering the rice fields. Looking at a carriage jumping in the dust ten feet away in front, we can imagine the autumn harvest scene in New Zealand. Sometimes three or five young military officers come galloping face to face like a race, and it will slightly cut through this quiet and indifferent realm, revealing an embarrassing disturbance. Really, I, who have always been accustomed to a comfortable life, do not envy command knives and medals. To be able to "pick chrysanthemums under the eastern fence and leisurely see the southern mountains," I cherish this "leisurely" feeling very much.

The coachman sits on the high pad pulling the reins, whipping the skinny horse again and again. Although there is a little regret, seeing the setting sun in the west and many Jiangbei children running and bowing behind the car to beg us for money, we feel calm after throwing some more copper coins.

The wind blows across our faces in the sunlight; there is already a hint of winter news. Pulling up our collars, we shiver and secretly recite the line: "The weather is already cool but not cold." Raising our eyes, we see a beautiful spire again on the distant Haitong mountain peak, silently exquisite, leaning against the clear autumn sky.

The riverside Shantang town also gradually falls into the cart canopy, and we get off the cart on a barren field under a stone bridge.

Tiger Hill is originally a mound, no more than one hundred and thirty feet high. Anyone who travels around will never develop a lover-like attachment to it; however, for me, although I have loved Tiantai, Yandang, Kuanglu, and Huangshan; at the same time, I also love a corner of the mountain and a shore of the water. I feel that Tiger Hill, like Yuantouzhu, is exquisite, quiet, and clean, like a quiet and virtuous female scholar. As before, in the dusk after a rain in mid-June, you step on the mountain steps paved with bricks and stones, and the verdant atmosphere on both sides flows out with a faint fragrance, so fresh that it sweetly intoxicates your heart, this is the characteristic of Tiger Hill. Moreover, the area is not large, and the structure is the most compact, with no gaps anywhere, but there is no place that is not high, refreshing, and magical.

We slipped into the mountain gate and walked up step by step. A little girl selling white orchids followed us step by step, wanting us to buy a few arrows from her. I fundamentally hate those turbid and strong fragrances, and shake my head at her, indicating that I don't want them, but she says in a pleading tone:

"Sir, buy Nu's arrow of flowers, three copper coins!"

That's right, she sells flowers for money, so I took out the copper coins and threw them into her flower basket, and explained to her why I didn't want that kind of annoyingly fragrant flower. However, she seemed embarrassed: "Then I'll lead you up!" she said. At that time, I felt that the unease that this person felt far exceeded what I felt. But I decided to decline her:

"No need to lead, we often come here to drink tea." I jumped onto the Tiger Hill shop with a reed shed. Then, I darted towards Lengxiang Pavilion. When I looked back on the stone steps, the little girl was hesitantly staring into the flower basket. My heart was heavy!.

Leaning on the stone railing, I roughly looked at the distant and near peaks, the clouds, smoke, bamboo, and trees at my feet, and then returned along the winding path lined with privet and green trees, passed the Dashe Guanyin Hall, and slipped down to see the Third Spring. This place is very similar to the Huanglong Cave of Kuanglu, but without a waterfall. Further down is the Jianchi, floating with a pool of duckweed-green spring water, without the meaning of "windy ravines and cloud springs". Looking up, there is a woman in red clothes walking over the stone bridge of the double buckets, which happens to be set off by the green vines and green leaves hanging in the two ravines. This figure is very small, truly a graceful and elegant painting. From here, proceed left on the remaining steps, walk past the Shuang Diaotong Bridge, and on that open space with weeds, the dilapidated Tiger Hill Pagoda stands on the right, and the strong and fresh Hufuge Pavilion sits on the left. In the wind window behind the Hufuge Pavilion, peering at the surrounding rice paddies, mountain trees, houses, fishermen, red frost maples, yellow tallow trees, and also mixed with unknown wild flowers of various colors under Haitong Peak, it is really very beautiful. (To be continued)

Records of Fragrant Incense Drifting 37

— Originally written by Princess Deling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

The candles used here are all very, very large, perhaps specially made, but in our eyes, accustomed to electric lights, the light is still very dim. Under this right-angled corridor, there are ten hanging on each of the three sides, but their hanging method is very special, which I have never seen before. Because what I have often seen before is either inserted into a candlestick on a table or hung on a candlestick on a wall, but here all lanterns are used. Lanterns are not a rare thing in themselves, I have seen thousands and hundreds of kinds of paper-covered and glass-encrusted ones, but I have never seen lanterns made of things like ox horns, and these horn lanterns are all made very thin, almost as transparent as glass. The products of Chinese handicrafts often have miracles that cannot be conceived by machinery, and this kind of horn lantern is an example.

The color of all the candles is bright red—other colors are considered unlucky, and of course, absolutely cannot be used. Each one is about a foot and a half long, which cannot be considered small, but the lantern itself is not very big, just enough to hold this candle. So I think it must be very difficult and dangerous to light it at first, and it may burn the lantern; but the eunuchs here have developed a very good technique, not only is it not difficult at all to light it at first, but there will never be any burning of the lantern—at least, during the few days I stayed in Fengtian, there never was. At the top of this horn lamp, three points are connected by a copper chain: in this way, the lamp can be stabilized. And at the end where these three copper chains are combined, there is also a copper hook. After the lamp wax is burning brightly, use this hook to hang it on the beam under the corridor, so that it hangs high. (180)

Page 17

Free Talk

The Cripple (by Zsigmond Móricz) 38

— Translated by Uncle Zhuang

Zsigmond Móricz is one of the most notable modern Hungarian authors. He excels at writing about the joyful countryside and simple, honest farmers. This short story effectively showcases his distinctive style. – Translator's note.

We arrived in the middle of the village.

Around us lay boundless wasteland. The plains were so uniform that we could only see the clear line of the horizon and the entire arc of the sky. In the exceptionally clear sky, large clouds floated, like joyful flags, bundles upon bundles of beautiful silk, hanging above you...

But my friend, he wasn't looking at the sky; his eyes, stern and cold, were fixed only on the ground. This land was his, about a thousand "acres" (approximately eight thousand mu - translator).

"It's such a nuisance!" he said. "It's such a nuisance to cultivate a thousand acres of land in this day and age! The value of agricultural products is at rock bottom, while the value of industrial goods is sky-high. People borrowed money, thinking they could easily repay it because wheat could sell for thirty-six 'pengos' (Hungarian currency - translator), but now wheat only sells for six 'pengos,' and the debt remains the same..."

He idly dug at the soil with his walking stick, this same soil that once yielded wheat worth thirty-six "pengos," just as fertile as before.

"What troubles you most are those damned short-term laborers. All they know is how to strike and demand higher wages... they don't care even if I lose money."

Resentfully, he sank back into his thoughts, then continued:

"But this year, I won't let those bastards make trouble. Last winter, I arranged it so that I only kept three and a half people. All the work is done by these three and a half people."

"How so?"

"It's very simple... In the autumn, I had them plow the land and sow wheat and rye. The rest, I leave to heaven to complete... As for livestock, I sold off the excess because I didn't have enough fodder stored up, and I certainly wasn't foolish enough to buy more. Besides, livestock is much cheaper to buy now than in the fall. I can now buy the livestock I need at a bargain price, so much so that it's hard to choose. In the winter, three people are more than enough to tend to the livestock and clean the livestock sheds."
