On Biting Words and Chewing Phrases 39

— Lin Lin

Writers, to vividly present their creations before the readers and capture their hearts, must first consider "What is the content?" Secondly, "How to express the content?" Here, we are saying that form is derived from content, and form is guided by content. At the same time, the quality of the form can also affect the content, which is a dialectical relationship. Therefore, writers need to skillfully and accurately describe their content, which is reality. Thus, the various problems in form cannot be ignored.

Since the problems in form cannot be ignored (and should be paid attention to), then we can establish a topic about biting words and chewing phrases within the problems of form. Of course, we are not saying to use a flowery and elaborate style, focusing solely on words, using colorful and ornate language to dazzle the readers' eyes. Without content, no matter how elaborate the form, it is difficult to gain value. There is a reason why the four-six parallel prose style has been relegated to the museum of antiquities. We always take realistic subject matter as the center of our content. Writers, to describe vividly and write realistically, needless to say, need to spend some effort to consider and study the use of language and words. The following will explain this in several points.

(1) In a work, the cleverness or clumsiness of a sentence or a word often affects the overall excellence of the work. There are many examples of this. For example, Song Qi wrote the line "A red apricot blooms, stirring up spring's delight," and because of the use of the word "stirring up," the entire scene is vividly presented before the reader's eyes. Being called the "Red Apricot" vice minister was not accidental.

(2) We do not approve of the kind of deliberation that Jia Dao engaged in, perhaps over the issue of elegance versus vulgarity. He hesitated between "a monk pushes the moonlit gate" and "a monk knocks on the moonlit gate." In our view—according to the principles of realistic methods—if the monk is pushing the gate, we use the word "push"; if he is knocking on the gate, we use the word "knock," describing the reality as it is, without any embellishment. However, if the monk is both pushing and knocking on the gate, it is no wonder that he spends so much effort on "pushing and knocking."

(3) The placement or inversion of words and phrases is also very important, often giving the reader very different or even opposite concepts. It is remembered that Zeng Guofan, in a certain period of resistance against the requested "Long Hair Bandits," once reported the war situation to the Qing Dynasty, and in his memorial, there was the sentence "repeated defeats after repeated battles." A staff member changed it to "repeated battles after repeated defeats," which turned the "incompetence" into "a spirit of struggling hard and having remaining courage to encourage." This kind of distortion of facts by biting words and chewing phrases is very harmful. Readers must compare it with the facts to see it.

(4) It is not advisable to dilute the original quality with too much water, like a drop of semen diluted in a lot of water. We should use the most economical and concise words and phrases to express the most complete and perfect concepts. For example, Lin Hejing's poem about a small plum tree in a mountain garden:

Sparse shadows slant across the clear, shallow water,

A faint fragrance drifts in the moonlit dusk.

He used only a few strokes, a light touch, but gave the reader a true and beautiful impression. It can be said that the author grasped the essence of reality and was able to visualize it with skillful techniques. These mere fourteen characters are better than a lengthy essay. Although the styles are different, the theory is entirely consistent. Here, we want to raise two more points: first, authors need to bite words and chew phrases in their expression; readers, when reading a work, also need to bite words and chew phrases, even putting themselves in the place of the author of the work, seeking what is expressed skillfully and what is presented well, so as to understand the truthfulness of the work's content. Second, we are not saying that authors should first master the skill of biting words and chewing phrases before writing. On the contrary, writing is needed to develop and refine the author's skill of biting words and chewing phrases, as well as other important techniques.

However, according to the above description, since biting words and chewing phrases has such important significance, how should writers use words and sentences to accurately grasp the concept of the content or vividly present the concept of the content? This question is difficult to answer, right? However, we can offer a few opinions. First, just as writers need to extract the main typical characters from all kinds of social groups, writers need to select typical words and sentences from all the words and sentences. Moreover, the more words and sentences the writer possesses, the more freedom of choice they have, and the more completely they can express themselves. Secondly, objective reality is evolving and becoming more complex day by day, and the tools for expressing this reality must also evolve and become more complex. Therefore, we not only cannot cling to old words and phrases that are easy to read and pleasing to the eye, but also should create some new words and phrases as much as possible, whether by accepting foreign words or adopting local dialects. In this way, not only can the tools themselves develop, but the expression of the content will also be more complete and satisfying. We cannot hesitate to try because of the "biting words and chewing phrases" and "nitpicking" of some nativists. We must know that if we do not start now, there will never be a day when it sounds smooth and looks pleasing to the eye. Most importantly, third: the theory of creation should use realistic methods, and we should use realistic methods in our use of words and sentences as well. Gorky said in his essay on creative technique: "A literary work, to be worthy of the name of art—must give the work a perfect verbal form. What gives this form to a story or novel is simple, correct, clear, and concise language."

Finally, what should be paid more attention to is: the importance of the issue is not in the biting words and chewing phrases in form—the deliberation of using words and sentences, which is just a small topic. The most important thing is that the writer must correctly understand objective reality, so that the creative life experience has richness, diversity, and truthfulness. Within this scope, our biting words and chewing phrases have meaning, and can give the subject matter a perfect artistic form.

X X X

College Students and Dancing 40

— Ding Shichang

If the newspapers hadn't published the news banning students from dancing, I really wouldn't have imagined that college students are actually the main patrons of dance halls. After this incident occurred, it attracted a lot of "public opinion." Recently, a gentleman analyzed the reasons why college students dance: (1) College students have money at home, (2) The social environment makes people feel bored, (3) Education is not done well, (4) Shanghai is too bad a place.

So the conclusion is that the current "dance ban policy" of various universities is a stopgap measure and will be difficult to achieve results: the fundamental solution lies in (1) Enriching the content of schools, (2) Finding ways to clarify social order to reduce people's boredom, (3) Giving less money to college students, (4) Promoting proper entertainment and games, (5) University professors leading by example, (6) Sanctions of public opinion; (7) Ballroom dancing can be encouraged, other dance forms should be despised.

Speaking of which, what is the current "dance ban policy" of various universities like? It is said that roll call is taken every night, and people are sent to the dance halls to investigate.

Needless to say, the dance ban policies of various universities will probably not have satisfactory results; however, the fundamental solutions involve such a large social environment that they may not be implemented immediately. For example, the last three reasons for the dancing craze cannot be solved piecemeal. For example, the fourth item, "Shanghai is too bad a place," is because Shanghai is an international city, and "international contradictions are all manifested here"; however, it is not known when Shanghai will be able to become a non-international Chinese city.

Even if Shanghai becomes a Chinese city, "contradictory phenomena"! Whether international or domestic, how can they not "be manifested here"?

In the past, Shanghai did not lack improper entertainment, there were plenty of brothels; in the past, there were also many children of wealthy people among Shanghai's college students; however, in the past, we didn't often hear about college students frequenting brothels, but now the dancing craze has become a problem. There is probably another reason in between. If you ask someone who often goes to dance halls, he will definitely blurt out the answer: because dancing is cheap and the procedures are simple, you can go in and dance a few times with a few dollars in your pocket.

This kind of cheap and simple improper "entertainment" can be said to be a kind of "modernization." And the creation of this "modernization" also has internal reasons in this country, that is, the bankruptcy of the rural economy, and too many women coming to the city to find work, the city cannot absorb them, and as a result, they have no choice but to sell their bodies.

Therefore, a small problem of college students dancing, if you get to the bottom of it, it will be terrible: college students dancing should be prohibited, but to deduce how to stop it without banning it, how to make those who want to dance have nowhere to dance, this is a very troublesome problem.

Innocent Child 41

— Li Chengxing

When the ××× Hospital telephoned my wife to inform her that the delivery was very safe, I felt very relaxed and happy. I immediately hired a rickshaw and went with Ah Bao: on the way, my thoughts were indeed not idle for half a moment. From today onwards, haven't I added another responsibility? If the infant had any knowledge, knowing that he would suffer extreme pain in this world in the future: that he would be subjected to all kinds of unreasonable ridicule by insidious people: also, that the whole world would only allow you to see the dark side, then, wouldn't the child curse me with a sharp voice? Ah, I am creating an innocent person to suffer in this world! I have committed a crime! "Parental love" is such a grand term, but who knows that the son's various pains are being given to him by his parents, these, the child has never known!

"Ah Bao, you have another younger brother!" I said, touching Ah Bao's head.

"It's fun to play with my younger brother, Dad, can you buy another foreign dog?" Ah Bao asked me, with an air as if his younger brother needed to play as soon as he was born.

When I arrived at the hospital, led by the nurse, I had already entered my wife's room. My wife was anxiously waiting for me on the bed, looking very tired, and it seemed to take all her strength to say a word.

"Don't you feel sad?" I asked about my wife's delivery.

"Where, it hurts a lot! Why didn't you come earlier."

"I didn't expect it to be so fast."

The baby's crying suddenly interrupted my conversation with my wife, and I immediately took him from the nurse's hand. The small life heavily pressed on my soul, because being a father is not just empty talk! The child's life, education, isn't it all handled by me alone?

"Let me see." My wife reached out her hand from the bed to take the child.

I immediately handed it over.

"Ah, ah." My wife touched the child's yellow and tender hair with satisfaction. At the same time, a loving gaze fell on the child.

In fact, my wife often said, "It's not good to have too many children. You have to teach them, you have to worry about them, and sometimes they are naughty, and you have to worry about their colds and fevers. Being a parent is like being half a horse!" But why is she so affectionate today? I was really a bit surprised. This must be the shining of a mother's love, right? This great maternal love must be surging in my wife's heart at this moment!

One evening after the birth, my wife and I joked.

"Fang, I've troubled you, don't ever again...!"

My wife folded her lips and finally laughed with a 'hee' sound.

At this time, the child's crying pierced into my heart again. So I thought again of the innocent child being pierced in his heart by a poisonous arrow again.

Elegy 42

— Zang Kejia

Like the cold shadow of a withered tree, this withering row, you further expand the gap of withering, pleasant past events are most afraid of coming to mind, but how can you ask me to close my memory tonight?

×　×　×　×

Peeling open the annual rings of the heart of the watchman, (your and my green section) a circle of endless smiling lines, covered with a layer of eternal darkness!

×　×　×　×

The family has no New Year from now on, sleeping through this New Year's morning with their heads covered, using a string of most taboo tears, to drip through ten thousand layers of joyful welcome.

×　×　×　×

On the banks of the Yellow River, far away, three thousand miles away, even if life and death are not different paths, a headless ghost may also have difficulty returning home.

Supplement to the Shanghai Shenbao

Brief Words

Death 57

— Chen Liang

Death is a very simple matter; when one can't catch one's breath, one dies.

There isn't a single creature in the world that doesn't die, so before the "elixir of immortality" is invented, all humans have no hope of living forever. The leaflets and policies of "wild ginseng" and "life insurance companies" do not state how long the life of the customer should be extended. Since death is inevitable for humans and cannot be avoided by anyone, it is not surprising that it is not feared by people.

However, the above refers to those who "die peacefully in their sleep." In today's world, in addition to dying peacefully in one's sleep, the number of people who die unnatural deaths is countless. Moreover, it is not uncommon for people to die unnatural deaths without knowing why. What does this so-called life security mean? I dare not say.

"If the King of Hell decrees death at the third watch, he will not let one live until the fifth watch." Assuming there really is a King of Hell, then the King of Hell should personally send a ghost to fetch one, so that one can "die with a clear conscience." However, some people are suddenly shot dead on the main road in broad daylight. The murderer is neither the King of Hell nor a ghost, but a living man. He can swagger in and swagger out, and he can calmly kill several people like killing chickens. The murdered people had no enemies or rivals in their lives, so does that mean that what controls human life is not in the "underworld" but in the "mortal world?"

Regardless of whether one dies at the hands of a ghost or at the hands of a fellow human being, things must be clear. The dead are gone, but the living deserve an explanation. "Come clean, go clear." Death is only a matter of time. Those who cause death today may have their lives taken by others in the future. The theory of karma, that "good is rewarded with good, and evil is rewarded with evil," has not been truly denied. It can be said that those who take other people's lives now may have their lives taken by others in the future. If people fight for life with life, the resulting loss will certainly belong to society.

In this way, death is indeed simple, but unnatural and inexplicable deaths are very complex.

Under today's circumstances, people do not hope for the invention of some "elixir of immortality," but are urgently seeking reliable "life security."

On Eradicating Corrupt Titles 58

— Wu Fei

Titles in our country have a realistic significance representing change, and from titles, one can discern class distinctions and the old or new mindset. For example, in the feudal era, there were "Xianggong," "Gongzi," "Shaoye," "Laoye," "Taitai," "Furen," "Xiaojie," "Nainai," and even "Yuanwai" and "Yuanjun." These not-so-familiar names can be found in old novels, like "slaves" and "inferior people." Students called their teachers "Fuzi" and referred to themselves as "Wansheng," sometimes adding "Daren." Here, one can fully see the differences in various classes and the strong feudal coloring. Now that it is the 20th century, with human enlightenment and material civilization, we have even been called "world people" (according to a certain book). Therefore, such corrupt titles are naturally not applicable. Moreover, according to the principle of human equality, there should not be any class distinctions in titles. However, in our country, the ancient and stubborn thinking has not been fundamentally eradicated to this day, so those outdated titles are still uttered in so-called aristocratic families or by those who protect the old ways. Of course, we cannot allow this remaining poison to exist. Although it does not cause much practical harm, it invisibly exposes the backwardness of the times and undermines the line of human equality, so it should be eliminated!

According to a Nanjing telegram in a certain newspaper on the 18th of this month: "The Ministry of the Interior has recently issued an order to all provinces to abolish corrupt titles such as 'Laoye,' 'Taitai,' 'Xiaojie,' 'Shaoye,' etc., to avoid being laughed at by foreign countries, and has ordered that in the future, everyone should be called 'Xiansheng,' 'Laoxiansheng,' or 'Xuesheng.'" Originally, the titles in our country were too complicated; just like dialects, not to mention the differences between provinces and regions, even within the same region, there are many similar but different titles, such as "Yeye," "Baba," "Die die," "Renxiong," "Laoxiong," "Laoge," etc.

Now that autocracy has been abolished, there is no possibility for class titles such as "Laoye," "Shaoye," "Taitai," "Xiaojie," etc. to exist. If we continue to use them, it is tantamount to admitting a restoration and returning to the era of feudal autocracy. We have the simple and reasonable "Xiansheng" available, why must we imitate feudal autocracy and pursue this kind of class-conscious title? I really don't understand. I think the most common and appropriate title is "Xiansheng," and for elders, it is acceptable to call them "Laoxiansheng." That kind of title is both equal and easy to say, regardless of class or status, from the Chairman of the National Government to laborers and servants, all can use it. Originally, titles are not the most important thing, but within a country, there should be uniformity.

From the abolition of corrupt titles, I also thought of writing letters: In ancient times, when writing letters in our country, people often used elaborate phrases and lengthy polite remarks, resulting in a long and tedious letter in which it was often difficult to find a few relevant and important words, and its emptiness and superficiality were self-evident. The person writing the letter had to be respectful and exhaust their brains, preparing to show off their talent to the other party, but the person reading the letter would get a headache and be confused. In the end, the important words would be weakened, and even things would be delayed. I think this kind of spirit that is useless to others and harmful to oneself is unnecessary: it is better to directly state the facts straightforwardly, make sure every word is meaningful, speak clearly, write clearly, be popular, be fluent, and don't forget to be concise. A few words are fine, and we don't object to either classical or vernacular Chinese.

We also have to find ways to correct these rigid and corrupt attitudes, just like abolishing corrupt titles.

Xiaoyao 59

— Xue

Small Words on a New Home 60

— Chi Yodai

It seems that my long-cherished wish has been fulfilled, being able to rent a small hut near the park. Naturally, it was a coincidence. A friend told me that there was such a hut suitable for me here, and the rent was unexpectedly cheap, which was the biggest issue. I had sacrificed a lot of time searching in this area like a hunting dog before, but all my efforts were in vain.

My luggage is so simple that I can set off two hours after deciding to move from this pier to that pier. Therefore, after crossing a few roads controlled by traffic lights, the landlord was surprised at how quickly I moved.

In a new environment, it seems that everything makes people excited. In fact, the reason is not that simple because I have realized my dream of several years. This can be illustrated by an example: regardless of the size of the matter, if you happen to buy a defective book at an old bookstore, and this defective book is exactly what you have not been able to find despite paying a high price, I know that you will be excited and satisfied all day, or even for a considerable amount of time.

Therefore, contrary to my previous habit of sleeping in, I am already looking out the window when the first sound in Shanghai rings out. Although it was late autumn when I moved, and now it is early winter, the morning wind seems to have a different kind of freshness, unlike the spring wind that is lazy, and unlike the summer wind that is cool. Every day, I experience the new feeling of this winter morning wind blowing on my body, but there are no fixed words to compare it to, and it has become a situation of both surprise and love.

The sky is just beginning to lighten, and the treetops in the park opposite are like a touch of Mi-style landscape painting, vaguely swaying in the wind. Occasionally, a few unknown sparrows chirp and sing. You must straighten your chest and take a deep, long breath. If you close your eyelids and meditate for a while, your body will feel somewhat ethereal.

However, this precious miracle is only a fleeting moment. When the landlord's servant pushes the door open and comes in, the world in front of you has changed.

This world: has ever-changing white clouds, has the rising sun with golden rays, has the sound of distant steam whistles... This world is moving.

Naturally, human life is moving. If you are forever immersed in a quiet world, you will become a cursing attitude to hate that fleeting precious miracle. But I didn't say not to want a moving world, I said the moving world is not as good as the quiet world. However, the number of people in the 3 million population who can watch this moving world transform into a disturbing world is unknown.

At this time, I wash my face and brush my teeth, and take a book to the park. Many times, I meet the little girl who delivers the newspaper at the door. In fact, taking books and newspapers to the park is not necessarily about choosing a place specifically to read seriously as if you were in a library. However, you whistle and stroll to the pond, and a vacant iron chair is waiting for you. Then sit down and spread the newspaper on the colored cover, casually turning to a page. You can look around as much as you like. A new clump of flowers has opened over there, a few small fish jump out of the water leisurely, or a familiar fellow nods to you with a smile. When your eyelids feel tired, then bring your gaze back to the newspaper to rest for a while. There may be a novel news item that makes you smile. Even flipping through a few illustrations or advertisements is quite meaningful. It is said that women are crutches, and newspapers may be able to serve this purpose for lonely people. What do you think?

When I go back, I exchange a bunch of flowers from an old flower seller. I know that putting them in my vase is cruel, but I have not used them as gifts to do something even more cruel, so I never feel guilty about it.

The Sound of Trains Haunts My Dreams Every Night 61

— Luo Jia

A cream-colored building stands isolated near the Beijing-Shanghai railway line. Its situation is lonely. Although there are flower-growing families nearby, the fields are full of purple, orange-yellow, scarlet, bright red, and unnamed flowers. These flowers will be transported to the wealthy families in the city as pure offerings on the table.

It must be a chance encounter! I lived in that cream-colored building as if in a dream. Every day, when I get up in the morning, a white-clothed waiter brings cheese cakes and a cup of oriental-flavored tea, carefully placing them on my dining table. When I return to the lounge, the empty shells of the Chesterfield cigarettes that I finished smoking last night are gone, and a newly opened can of Three Cannon Towers is placed there instead. Therefore, I sit quietly on the velvet sofa and smoke.

Life is leisurely and wealthy. Naturally, the person who persuaded me to come to this cream-colored building has great expectations, because I am a young man, and young people love strength, love heat, and also love light. Therefore, my previous life was hot and prickly. However, when that kind of hot and prickly life could no longer continue, my lifestyle changed and became gray, decadent, and wandering. Because of this, I was forced into this cream-colored building. Their intention is to hope that I can rest quietly for a year and, through quiet self-reflection, put my life back on track.

Page 21

Perhaps their self-righteous plan will be fruitless, because in my heart, there is a southern swallow that flies in and out, but never wants to stay for a moment. Therefore, my heart is afraid of being disheartened. In that case, making life a little more regular is not an easy thing.

Every moment, I sit quietly in this cream-colored building, listening to the trains coming from Nanjing and going to Shanghai, sounding with deafening noise, getting closer to my ears, and then farther away!

However, at night, even a strand of white hair falling on a red leather book can be heard with a loud sound, and every sound, every time, stirs my heartstrings, reminding me of the dream-like days of the past, the dream-like, colorful deeds in the dream-like days.

However, when I fall into a peaceful sleep, I am awakened by the shrill sound of train whistles, and the sweet, sour, bitter, and spicy flavors in my dream fade away in my weak memory! No matter how hard I try to repeat and patch them together for a long night, they are still incomplete, aren't they? However, every night, I am dreaming a string of incomplete dreams!

East, West, South, North 62

— Sanduo

Lu Wenqing, a young man from Henan, turned to a life of depravity and theft due to the pain of unemployment after graduating from university. He was sentenced to four months in prison as a warning after the matter was discovered.

Not my friend Hu Shi's conversation with a reporter from the Beijing Daily News. I, who am teaching at Peking University, have seen many university graduates. Except for a very small number of special cases, most of them can find considerable jobs after graduation... Therefore, if you want to work happily and have no worries about unemployment, the first thing you must have is the ability and knowledge to do the job... Those who cannot find employment should seek the reasons why they cannot find employment, and do not need to complain about the world and blame others, but only blame themselves. If you have the ability, why worry about not having food to eat...

This is the doctor's opinion. Naturally, it is very measured. A university student like Lu Wenqing is probably something that the doctor, while eating fancy food and smoking cigars, would never dream of. "You reap what you sow!" Does the doctor think so?

However, it is indeed a fact. The editor of the newspaper does not necessarily deliberately create rumors. Then, borrowing the doctor's conclusion, "As for the relief of unemployment, it is another kind of social problem. It is also the responsibility of society to provide jobs for the unemployed."

Sketches of Dance Hall Figures 63

— Xiaolin

Many women who drifted away from their men's teams revealed their vulgar faces that were usually decorated. Seeing a female companion sitting on the other side, they ran over and danced lightly with the companion's man's arm around their waist under the dark green light. It was as if it wouldn't hurt their own men at all. Without any reservations. If men did the same: eagerly going to the table of someone else's female companion who has a man, the reaction would be different. Even if they didn't say any dissatisfied words, there was no need to convey the meaning with sound. The sudden change of face was a clear indication of extreme dissatisfaction. It goes without saying that there was even more discord in their hearts.

The selfish thoughts peculiar to women are easily expressed unconsciously at certain times. They may have a temporary hugging relationship with other men, but they do not allow men to have contact with other women. Approximately every woman is inevitable of this unconscious thought. They worry that the temporary hugging relationship will develop into entanglements that go beyond temporality. If that becomes a fact, it is equivalent to a robbery of their own love, so they have this preventive behavior to prevent accidents. However, if a man's feelings may overflow beyond ordinary social interactions, then a woman's feelings may naturally also have the same overflowing effect. Because the emotional intrusion between people is of the same form. But few men have measured up to this. Letting their women dance with friends is a very ordinary occasion. But they don't trust others so much that they even obstruct the woman's freedom of action, which is a social courtesy. The inferiority of women to men can be seen from these places. Due to a certain terrible illusion created by the heart, their spirits are constantly troubled by this illusion. And especially when mixed in a dance hall with more men, that illusion will become increasingly thick. Before a glimpse, their mood was still full of joy and delight. Perhaps after a moment, their mood will change greatly. Joy and delight quickly sink. And the whole thing is shrouded in unwarranted worries. If a man accidentally opens his mouth a few more times or shows a little more smile while dancing with another woman, the feeling given to the woman will be even more painful, unbearable, and even lead to the sadness of seeming to be forgotten.

Women have a narrow heart that men do not have. Therefore, the troubles they attract are indeed more numerous and more harmful than those of men. Some things do not need to be taken so seriously, and do not need to be thought about so much. However, women always like to not take things so seriously, and not think so much. They worry about things that don't need to be worried about. Then all kinds of meaningless torments are self-inflicted. However, if men see through this state of mind of women and don't want to call women to be entangled in the net of suffering created by themselves. It is better to do less of those actions that can be reduced, and only dance with their own women, and not dance with any other women, which is a loss for women to suffer for no reason. Therefore, single men are more lonely guarding the table than single women are. Women's emotions are truly incredible, just like silkworms binding themselves. They spit out silk, form cocoons, and then put themselves in the cocoons. They originally went to a place with a full sense of enthusiasm. When they get to the place, they don't know why they disappear, and they feel disappointed, annoyed, and even regret coming out. Especially in the dance hall, women cannot completely hide this expression of joys and sorrows, which is displayed in front of men.

Women's hearts are fragile and small after all.

The Cries of Mice 64

— Jing Jia

Cruel people, why do you use such terrible means to deal with us? You curse us, hate us, and spare no effort to use your brains to manufacture all kinds of machines to capture us every day, as if you won't give up until the mice are extinct. Why is it like this? We are the same animals, with the same blood and flesh!

You often scold us for being bastards, saying that we shouldn't bite the objects in the house or steal the food you store. This seems to be the crime for which we are to be sentenced to death! But we also have unavoidable difficulties. Why not give us some time to defend ourselves before imposing cruel punishments?

You should believe that a person who can maintain their own life is never willing to be a thief. At the same time, solving the problem of livelihood is an instinct that all living things have. We are also one of the living things! We know hunger, and we know how to find food to relieve our hunger. This is nature, and nature cannot be changed by human power. People can find something to eat when they are hungry, so why can't we? Why do we have to be sentenced to death for finding food?

Let's talk about biting things. We are also forced to do this. Our teeth grow very quickly. If we don't bite things, our teeth can drill out of our lips in a few days. In order to prevent this unfortunate event, we certainly have to bite things to wear down their growth. This is the same as people using their brains. If you don't use your brains, your brains will degenerate. In order to make your brains develop, you have to use them. This is the truth of nature. Why can you apply the truth, but we are punished for the truth?

It's too unfair, really, too unfair! God created humans, and God created us. God did not specify that humans can arbitrarily slaughter us. We have the same freedom to exist. The Earth belongs to all living things. Who can say that the world is solely owned by humans?

Storytelling 66

Yao Xiao'an Pang Xueqing Pearl Pagoda

China and West (1040) 10:00 AM to 11:00 AM

Opening: "Reed Forest"

Deep in the reed forest, birds startle and fly. The mist is thin and the smoke is light, obscuring the view. Five carts of books are enough for three winters. Jiang Xiuru strolls idly with nothing to do. In the reeds, he hears cries. It is the wife of Pang, the Third Daughter. Third Daughter appears. She stops crying. She calls out to Jiang Lang, "Please wait!" She says, "I am not virtuous, I have violated the way of a wife." She also says, "I don't understand and have deceived you with hidden intentions." Today, it must be clear whether it is right or wrong. "Oh, I have befriended neighbors as relatives, kept track of how many families had how many items of clothing, cursed my mother-in-law who passed away early. How can I excuse these three unfilial offenses? " Jiang Lang, I read the "Instructions for Women" in my youth. I know a thing or two about the great rituals and constant virtues. Serving my mother-in-law is my duty. Even if people don't know, Heaven knows. I hope Jiang Lang will take me home. Remember when we were a married couple? An'an is young. Don't deceive me, but don't deceive our child." Jiang immediately felt a sense of misery upon hearing this. But how could he dare defy his mother's orders? "Let me first go back and report in detail. If mother agrees, I will take in An'an and then fetch you, my wife."

National Studies 68

Ms. Wang Bingmei's Tang Poetry

Hua Xing (1260) 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM

Sent to Han, Advisor to the Emperor

I am not happy now, I think of Yueyang.

My body wants to fly, but I am sick in bed.

Beautiful women are separated by the autumn water.

Washing their feet in Dongting, gazing at the vast wilderness.

Wild geese fly in the dark, the sun and moon are white.

Red maple leaves, the sky rains frost.

The Jade Capital, a group of emperors gather at the Big Dipper.

Some ride unicorns, shaded by phoenixes.

Lotus banners, smoke and mist fall.

Shadows move, reflecting the upside-down scenery of Xiao and Xiang.

The star palace lords are drunk on fine wine.

Feathered men are few and not by their side.

It seems I heard that yesterday, Red Pine Master

Is probably Han Zhangzi of the Han Dynasty.

In the past, he followed the Liu clan to secure Chang'an.

The tent has not changed, but his spirit is sadly wounded.

How dare I discuss the success or failure of the nation?

Although my color is tainted and decaying, I eat maple fragrance.

Staying in Zhou Nan is a pity of ancient times.

Old Xin in the South Pole should be long-lived and prosperous.

Beautiful women, why are you separated by the autumn water?

How can you be placed in the jade hall of tribute?

Old Cypress Tree - Du Fu

In front of Zhuge Liang's temple, there is an old cypress tree.

Its branches are like bronze, and its roots are like stone.

Its bark is slippery with rain, forty spans around.

Its dark green color reaches the sky, two thousand feet tall.

Clouds come and its breath connects with the Wuxia Gorge.

The moon rises and its coldness connects with the white snow mountain.

The ruler and his minister have already met with the times.

The trees are still cherished by people.

I remember yesterday, winding around the east of Jinting Pavilion.

The First Ruler and Martial Marquis were buried in the same palace.

The towering branches and trunks are ancient in the suburbs.

The secluded and graceful painted doors and windows are empty.

Although it is situated well, it is isolated.

Lonely and high in the dark, it often faces strong winds.

It is supported by the power of the gods.

Its uprightness is originally due to the work of creation.

If the great building is about to collapse, it needs beams and pillars.

The yellow ox turns its head and the hills are heavy.

It does not reveal its literary talent, yet the world is already amazed.

Who can send it away if it does not decline pruning?

How can a bitter heart avoid accommodating ants?

Fragrant leaves will eventually lightly house luan and phoenixes.

Do not complain, ambitious scholars and hermits,

Since ancient times, great talents have been difficult to use.
